        % Value changed function: SelecionarEixoDropDown
        function SelecionarEixoDropDownValueChanged(app, event)
            if(string(app.SelecionarEixoDropDown.Value) == string('Selecionar'))
                cla(app.UIAxes);
                cla(app.UIAxes_2);
                app.DimetrodoEixoEditField.Value = '';
                app.TorqueMximoEditField.Value = '';
                app.MomentoMximoEditField.Value = '';
                app.SelecionarElementoDropDown.Visible = 'off';
                app.SelecionarElementoDropDownLabel.Visible = 'off';
                app.FxEditField.Visible = 'off';
                app.FyEditField.Visible = 'off';
                app.FzEditField.Visible = 'off';
                app.FxEditField_2Label.Visible = 'off';
                app.FyEditFieldLabel.Visible = 'off';
                app.FzEditFieldLabel.Visible = 'off';
                app.FxEditField.Value = '';
                app.FyEditField.Value = '';
                app.FzEditField.Value = '';
            end
            if(not(string(app.SelecionarEixoDropDown.Value) == string('Selecionar')))
                nomes = [];
                for i=1:length(app.butte)
                    nomes = [nomes string(app.butte(i).Text)];
                end
                ind = find(nomes == string(app.SelecionarEixoDropDown.Value));
                app.exf=ind;
                
                if(app.sistema == 1)
                    uni1 = 'mm';
                    uni2 = 'Nm';
                elseif(app.sistema == 0)
                    uni1 = 'pol';
                    uni2 = 'lbf.pol';
                end
                app.DimetrodoEixoEditField.Value = [sprintf('%.2f ', app.de(ind)) uni1];
                app.TorqueMximoEditField.Value = [sprintf('%.1f ', app.Tmax(ind)) uni2];
                app.MomentoMximoEditField.Value = [sprintf('%.1f ',app.Mrmax(ind)) uni2];
                
                % Plotando os graficos de momento
                
                cla(app.UIAxes);
                cla(app.UIAxes_2);
                minplot = 0;
                maxplot = 0;
                for i=1:size(app.M{ind},2)
                    if(app.sistema == 1)
                        plot(app.UIAxes,1000*app.M{ind}{1,i},app.M{ind}{2,i},'k')
                    elseif(app.sistema == 0)
                        plot(app.UIAxes,app.M{ind}{1,i},app.M{ind}{2,i},'k')
                    end
                    hold(app.UIAxes, 'on')
                    if(i<size(app.M{ind},2))
                        if(app.M{ind}{2,i}(100)~=app.M{ind}{2,i+1}(1))
                            if(app.sistema == 1)
                                plot(app.UIAxes, [1000*app.M{ind}{1,i}(100),app.M{ind}{1,i+1}(1)],[1000*app.M{ind}{2,i}(100),app.M{ind}{2,i+1}(1)],'k')
                            elseif(app.sistema == 0)
                                plot(app.UIAxes, [app.M{ind}{1,i}(100),app.M{ind}{1,i+1}(1)],[app.M{ind}{2,i}(100),app.M{ind}{2,i+1}(1)],'k')
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if(app.M{ind}{2,1}(1)~=0)
                        if(app.sistema == 1)
                            plot(app.UIAxes, [1000*app.M{ind}{1,1}(1),1000*app.M{ind}{1,1}(1)],[0,app.M{ind}{2,1}(1)],'k','LineWidth',2)
                        elseif(app.sistema == 0)
                            plot(app.UIAxes, [app.M{ind}{1,1}(1),app.M{ind}{1,1}(1)],[0,app.M{ind}{2,1}(1)],'k','LineWidth',2)
                        end
                    end
                    if(minplot>min(app.M{ind}{2,i}))
                        minplot = min(app.M{ind}{2,i});
                    end
                    if(maxplot<max(app.M{ind}{2,i}))
                        maxplot = max(app.M{ind}{2,i});
                    end
                end
                xlimmin=min([app.M{ind}{1,1}(1) app.M{ind}{1,size(app.M{ind},2)}(101)]);
                xlimmax=max([app.M{ind}{1,1}(1) app.M{ind}{1,size(app.M{ind},2)}(101)]);
                if(app.sistema == 1)
                    xlim(app.UIAxes, 1000*[xlimmin xlimmax])
                elseif(app.sistema == 0)
                    xlim(app.UIAxes, [xlimmin xlimmax])
                end
                
                if(minplot~=maxplot)
                    ylim(app.UIAxes, [minplot maxplot]);
                else
                    ylim(app.UIAxes, [-1 1]);
                end
                grid(app.UIAxes, 'on')
                xlabel(app.UIAxes, sprintf('Posição (%s)',uni1))
                ylabel(app.UIAxes, sprintf('Momento (%s)',uni2))
                if(app.dire{1}(3) == 3)
                    labelg1 = 'ZX';
                    labelg2 = 'ZY';
                elseif(app.dire{1}(3) == 1)
                    labelg1 = 'XY';
                    labelg2 = 'XZ';
                elseif(app.dire{1}(3) == 2)
                    labelg1 = 'YZ';
                    labelg2 = 'YX';
                end
                    
                title(app.UIAxes, ['Momento fletor no plano ' labelg1])
                
                minplot = 0;
                maxplot = 0;
                for i=1:size(app.M{ind},2)
                    if(app.sistema == 1)
                        plot(app.UIAxes_2, 1000*app.M{ind}{1,i},app.M{ind}{3,i},'k')
                    elseif(app.sistema == 0)
                        plot(app.UIAxes_2, app.M{ind}{1,i},app.M{ind}{3,i},'k')
                    end
                    hold(app.UIAxes_2, 'on')
                    if(i<size(app.M{ind},2))
                        if(app.M{ind}{3,i}(100)~=app.M{ind}{3,i+1}(1))
                            if(app.sistema == 1)
                                plot(app.UIAxes_2, [1000*app.M{ind}{1,i}(100),1000*app.M{ind}{1,i+1}(1)],[app.M{ind}{3,i}(100),app.M{ind}{3,i+1}(1)],'k')
                            elseif(app.sistema == 0)
                                plot(app.UIAxes_2, [app.M{ind}{1,i}(100),app.M{ind}{1,i+1}(1)],[app.M{ind}{3,i}(100),app.M{ind}{3,i+1}(1)],'k')
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if(app.M{ind}{3,1}(1)~=0)
                        if(app.sistema == 1)
                            plot(app.UIAxes_2, [1000*app.M{ind}{1,1}(1),1000*app.M{ind}{1,1}(1)],[0,app.M{ind}{3,1}(1)],'k','LineWidth',2)
                        elseif(app.sistema == 0)
                            plot(app.UIAxes_2, [app.M{ind}{1,1}(1),app.M{ind}{1,1}(1)],[0,app.M{ind}{3,1}(1)],'k','LineWidth',2)
                        end
                    end
                    if(minplot>min(app.M{ind}{3,i}))
                        minplot = min(app.M{ind}{3,i});
                    end
                    if(maxplot<max(app.M{ind}{3,i}))
                        maxplot = max(app.M{ind}{3,i});
                    end
                end
                if(app.sistema == 1)
                    xlim(app.UIAxes_2, ([1000*xlimmin 1000*xlimmax]))
                elseif(app.sistema == 0)
                    xlim(app.UIAxes_2, ([xlimmin xlimmax]))
                end
                
                if(minplot~=maxplot)
                    ylim(app.UIAxes_2, [minplot maxplot]);
                else
                    ylim(app.UIAxes_2, [-1 1]);
                end
                grid(app.UIAxes_2, 'on')
                xlabel(app.UIAxes_2, sprintf('Posição (%s)',uni1))
                ylabel(app.UIAxes_2, sprintf('Momento (%s)',uni2))
                title(app.UIAxes_2, ['Momento fletor no plano ' labelg2])
                app.FxEditField.Visible = 'on';
                app.FyEditField.Visible = 'on';
                app.FzEditField.Visible = 'on';
                app.SelecionarElementoDropDown.Visible = 'on';
                app.SelecionarElementoDropDownLabel.Visible = 'on';
                app.FxEditField_2Label.Visible = 'on';
                app.FyEditFieldLabel.Visible = 'on';
                app.FzEditFieldLabel.Visible = 'on';
                refeng=[];
                for(ne=1:length(app.refe))
                    if(ind == app.refe{ne}(1) || ind == app.refe{ne}(3))
                        refeng(length(refeng)+1)=ne;
                    end
                end
                textdrop = {'Selecionar','Mancal 1','Mancal 2'};
                for i=1:length(refeng)
                    textdrop{length(textdrop)+1} = char(sprintf('Engrenagens %d',refeng(i)));
                end
                app.SelecionarElementoDropDown.Items = textdrop;
            end
            
        end

                    if(string(app.AdicionarEixoPanel.Visible) == string('on'))
                        atualizareixoeng(app)
                    end
                end
            end  
        end

        % Value changed function: SelecionarElementoDropDown
        function SelecionarElementoDropDownValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.SelecionarElementoDropDown.Value;
            e=app.exf;
            if(not(string(value) == string('Selecionar')))
                if(string(value) == string('Mancal 1'))
                    if(app.sistema == 1)
                        app.FxEditField.Value = sprintf('%.3f kN',app.fm{(e-1)*2+1}(1)/1000);
                        app.FyEditField.Value = sprintf('%.3f kN',app.fm{(e-1)*2+1}(2)/1000);
                        app.FzEditField.Value = sprintf('%.3f kN',app.fm{(e-1)*2+1}(3)/1000);
                    elseif(app.sistema == 0)
                        app.FxEditField.Value = sprintf('%.2f lbf',app.fm{(e-1)*2+1}(1));
                        app.FyEditField.Value = sprintf('%.2f lbf',app.fm{(e-1)*2+1}(2));
                        app.FzEditField.Value = sprintf('%.2f lbf',app.fm{(e-1)*2+1}(3));
                    end
                elseif(string(value) == string('Mancal 2'))
                    if(app.sistema == 1)
                        app.FxEditField.Value = sprintf('%.3f kN',app.fm{(e-1)*2+2}(1)/1000);
                        app.FyEditField.Value = sprintf('%.3f kN',app.fm{(e-1)*2+2}(2)/1000);
                        app.FzEditField.Value = sprintf('%.3f kN',app.fm{(e-1)*2+2}(3)/1000);
                    elseif(app.sistema == 0)
                        app.FxEditField.Value = sprintf('%.2f lbf',app.fm{(e-1)*2+2}(1));
                        app.FyEditField.Value = sprintf('%.2f lbf',app.fm{(e-1)*2+2}(2));
                        app.FzEditField.Value = sprintf('%.2f lbf',app.fm{(e-1)*2+2}(3));
                    end
                else
                    nomes = [];
                    for i=1:length(app.butt)
                        nomes = [nomes string(app.butt(i).Text)];
                    end
                    ind = find(nomes == string(sprintf('%s ',value)));
                    if(e == app.refe{ind}(1))
                        engs=app.refe{ind}(2);
                    elseif(e == app.refe{ind}(3))
                        engs=app.refe{ind}(4);
                    end
                    if(app.sistema == 1)
                        app.FxEditField.Value = sprintf('%.3f kN',app.f{e}{engs}(1)/1000);
                        app.FyEditField.Value = sprintf('%.3f kN',app.f{e}{engs}(2)/1000);
                        app.FzEditField.Value = sprintf('%.3f kN',app.f{e}{engs}(3)/1000);
                    elseif(app.sistema == 0)
                        app.FxEditField.Value = sprintf('%.2f lbf',app.f{e}{engs}(1));
                        app.FyEditField.Value = sprintf('%.2f lbf',app.f{e}{engs}(2));
                        app.FzEditField.Value = sprintf('%.2f lbf',app.f{e}{engs}(3));
                    end
                end

            end
                        
                
        end

        % Button pushed function: AnliseDinmicaButton
        function AnliseDinmicaButtonPushed(app, event)
            app.PanelResultado.Visible = 'off';
            app.AnaliseDinamica.Visible = 'on';
            app.EngrenagensdeDentesRetosPanel.Visible = 'off';
            
            if(length(app.nomee) == 0)
                app.SelecionarEixoDropDown.Items = {'Selecionar'};
            else
                textdrop = {'Selecionar'};
                for i=1:length(app.nomee)
                    textdrop{length(textdrop)+1} = char(app.nomee(i));
                end
                for i=1:length(app.nomeex)
                    textdrop{length(textdrop)+1} = char(app.nomeex(i));
                end
                app.ElementosDropDown.Items = textdrop;
            end
            
            app.ElementosDropDown.Value = 'Selecionar';
            
        end

        % Value changed function: ElementosDropDown
        function ElementosDropDownValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.ElementosDropDown.Value;
            veng=[];
            veng2=[];
            if(not(string(value) == "Selecionar"))
                for(i=1:length(app.nomee))
                    if(value == string(app.nomee(i)))
                        veng=i;
                        break
                    end
                end
                for(i=1:length(app.nomeex))
                    if(value == string(app.nomeex(i)))
                        veng2=i;
                        break
                    end
                end
                if(length(veng)>0)
                    vex=app.refe{veng}(1);
                    vpeg=app.refe{veng}(2);
                    if(string(app.tipoe{vex}(vpeg)) == "Dentes Retos")
                        app.EngrenagensdeDentesRetosPanel.Visible = 'on';
                        app.EixosPanel.Visible='off';
                        app.EngrenagensdeDentesRetosPanel.Title = 'Engrenagens de Dentes Retos';
                    end
                    if(string(app.tipoe{vex}(vpeg)) == "Helicoidal")
                        app.EngrenagensdeDentesRetosPanel.Visible = 'on';
                        app.EngrenagensdeDentesRetosPanel.Title = 'Engrenagens de Dentes Helicoidais';
                    end
                end
                if(length(veng2)>0)
                    app.EixosPanel.Visible='on';
                    app.EngrenagensdeDentesRetosPanel.Visible = 'off';
                end
            else
                app.EngrenagensdeDentesRetosPanel.Visible = 'off';
            end
        end

        % Value changed function: MaterialdacoroaDropDown
        function MaterialdacoroaDropDownValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Value;
            app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Enable = 'on';
            app.EdacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'off';
            app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Enable = 'on';
            if(string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{1}))
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {''};
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {'Endurecido por completo' 'Endurecido por chama ou indução' 'Carbonetado e endurecido' 'Nitretado (aços endurecidos por completo)' 'Outro'};
            elseif(string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{2}) || string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{3}) || string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{4}))
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {''};
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {'Nitretado (aços endurecidos por completo)' 'Outro'};
            elseif(string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{5}))
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {''};
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {'Recozido' 'Outro'};
            elseif(string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{6}) || string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{7}))
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {''};
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {'Temperado e revenido' 'Outro'};
            elseif(string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{8}) || string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{9}) || string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{10}))
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {''};
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {'Como fundido' 'Outro'};
            elseif(string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{11}))
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {''};
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {'Fundido em areia' 'Outro'};
            elseif(string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{12}))
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {''};
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {'Tratado termicamente' 'Outro'};
            elseif(string(value)==string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items{13}))
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items = {'Outro'};
                app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Enable = 'off';
                app.EdacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'on';
                app.ScadacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'on';
                app.StadacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'on';
            end
            if(not(string(app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Value) == "Outro"))
                app.ScadacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'off';
                app.StadacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'off';
            end
            value2 = string(app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Value);
            value1 = string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Value);
            item2 = app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items;
            item1 = app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items;
            app.ScadacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'off';
            app.StadacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'off';
            app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Items = {''};
            if(string(value2)=="Outro")
                app.ScadacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'on';
                app.StadacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'on';
                app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Enable = 'off';
            else
                app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Enable = 'on';
                if(value1==string(item1{1}))
                    if(value2==string(item2{1}) || value2==string(item2{2}) || value2==string(item2{3})) 
                        app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Items = {'1' '2'};
                    elseif(value2==string(item2{4}) || value2==string(item2{5}))
                        app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Items = {'1' '2' '3'};
                    else
                        app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Enable = 'off';
                    end
                elseif(value1==string(item1{2}) || value1==string(item1{3}) || value1==string(item1{4}))
                    if(value2==string(item2{1}))
                        app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Items = {'1' '2' '3'};
                    else
                        app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Enable = 'off';
                    end
                else
                    app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Enable = 'off';
                end     
            end
            mudarscc(app);
            mudarec(app);
        end

        % Value changed function: TrattrmicocoroaDropDown
        function TrattrmicocoroaDropDownValueChanged(app, event)
            value2 = string(app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Value);
            value1 = string(app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Value);
            item2 = app.TrattrmicocoroaDropDown.Items;
            item1 = app.MaterialdacoroaDropDown.Items;
            app.ScadacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'off';
            app.StadacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'off';
            app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Items = {''};
            if(string(value2)=="Outro")
                app.ScadacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'on';
                app.StadacoroapsiEditField.Enable = 'on';
                app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Enable = 'off';
            else
                app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Enable = 'on';
                if(value1==string(item1{1}))
                    if(value2==string(item2{1}) || value2==string(item2{2})) 
                        app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Items = {'1' '2'};
                    elseif(value2==string(item2{3}) || value2==string(item2{4}))
                        app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Items = {'1' '2' '3'};
                    else
                        app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Enable = 'off';
                    end
                elseif(value1==string(item1{2}) || value1==string(item1{3}) || value1==string(item1{4}))
                    if(value2==string(item2{1}))
                        app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Items = {'1' '2' '3'};
                    else
                        app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Enable = 'off';
                    end
                else
                    app.GraudacoroaDropDown.Enable = 'off';
                end     
            end
            mudarscc(app);
        end

        % Value changed function: TrattrmicopinhoDropDown
        function TrattrmicopinhoDropDownValueChanged(app, event)
            value2 = string(app.TrattrmicopinhoDropDown.Value);
            value1 = string(app.MaterialdopinhoDropDown.Value);
            item2 = app.TrattrmicopinhoDropDown.Items;
            item1 = app.MaterialdopinhoDropDown.Items;
            app.ScadopinhopsiEditField.Enable = 'off';
            app.StadopinhopsiEditField.Enable = 'off';
            app.GraudopinhoDropDown.Items = {''};
            if(string(value2)=="Outro")
                app.ScadopinhopsiEditField.Enable = 'on';
                app.StadopinhopsiEditField.Enable = 'on';
                app.GraudopinhoDropDown.Enable = 'off';
            else
                app.GraudopinhoDropDown.Enable = 'on';
                if(value1==string(item1{1}))
                    if(value2==string(item2{1}) || value2==string(item2{2})) 
                        app.GraudopinhoDropDown.Items = {'1' '2'};
                    elseif(value2==string(item2{3}) || value2==string(item2{4}))
                        app.GraudopinhoDropDown.Items = {'1' '2' '3'};
                    else
                        app.GraudopinhoDropDown.Enable = 'off';
                    end
                elseif(value1==string(item1{2}) || value1==string(item1{3}) || value1==string(item1{4}))
                    if(value2==string(item2{1}))
                        app.GraudopinhoDropDown.Items = {'1' '2' '3'};
                    else
                        app.GraudopinhoDropDown.Enable = 'off';
                    end
                else
                    app.GraudopinhoDropDown.Enable = 'off';
                end     
            end
            mudarscp(app);
        end

        % Value changed function: CaractdoaroDropDown
        function CaractdoaroDropDownValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.CaractdoaroDropDown.Value;
            app.MbEditField.Enable = 'off';
            if(string(value)==string(app.CaractdoaroDropDown.Items{2}))
                app.MbEditField.Enable = 'on';
                app.MbEditField.Value = 1;
            else
                app.MbEditField.Value = 1.2;
            end
        end

        % Button pushed function: RelatrioButton
        function RelatrioButtonPushed(app, event)
            if(app.sistema == 0)
                unid=' lbf';
                unid2=' in';
                unid3=' lbf.in';
            else
                unid=' N';
                unid2=' mm';
                unid3=' N.m';
            end
            fileID = fopen('relatorio.txt','w');
            fprintf(fileID,'=======================================================\n');
            fprintf(fileID,'                        RELATÓRIO                      \n');
            fprintf(fileID,'=======================================================\n\n');
            if(length(app.nomeex))==0
                fprintf(fileID,'Nenhum elemento foi declarado\n\n');
            else
                fprintf(fileID,'ANÁLISE ESTÁTICA:\n\n');
                if(length(app.nomeex)>0)
                    for i=1:length(app.nomeex)
                        fprintf(fileID,'======= %s =======\n\n',app.nomeex(i));
                        if(length(app.de)<i || (length(app.de)>=i && app.de(i)==0))
                            fprintf(fileID,'Nenhum elemento declarado no %s \n\n', app.nomeex(i));
                        end
                        if(length(app.de)>=i)
                            if(app.de(i)>0)
                                fprintf(fileID,'Diâmetro mínimo: %.2f%s\n',app.de(i),unid2);
                                fprintf(fileID,'Torque máximo: %.2f%s\n',app.Tmax(i),unid3);
                                fprintf(fileID,'Momento máximo: %.2f%s\n\n',app.Mrmax(i),unid3);
                                
                                for j=(i-1)*2+1:(i-1)*2+2
                                    fprintf(fileID,'Reação no Mancal %d:\n\n',j-(i-1)*2);
                                    fprintf(fileID,'Fx = %.3f%s\n',app.fm{j}(1),unid);
                                    fprintf(fileID,'Fy = %.3f%s\n',app.fm{j}(2),unid);
                                    fprintf(fileID,'Fz = %.3f%s\n\n',app.fm{j}(3),unid);
                                end
                                for j=1:length(app.f{i})
                                    for k=1:length(app.refe)
                                        if((i==app.refe{k}(1) && j==app.refe{k}(2)) || (i==app.refe{k}(3) && j==app.refe{k}(4)))
                                            ref=k;
                                            break
                                        end
                                    end
                                    fprintf(fileID,'Forças nas %s:\n\n',app.nomee(ref));
                                    fprintf(fileID,'Fx = %.3f%s\n',app.f{i}{j}(1),unid);
                                    fprintf(fileID,'Fy = %.3f%s\n',app.f{i}{j}(2),unid);
                                    fprintf(fileID,'Fz = %.3f%s\n\n',app.f{i}{j}(3),unid);
                                end
                                
                            end
                        end  
                    end
                end
                fprintf(fileID,'===================================\n\n');
                fprintf(fileID,'ANÁLISE DINÂMICA:\n\n');
                if(isempty(app.dinamica) && isempty(app.dinamicae))
                    fprintf(fileID,'Nenhuma análise dinâmica foi executada\n\n');
                else
                    dina=[];
                    dina2=[];
                    if(length(app.dinamica)>0)
                        for i=1:length(app.dinamica)
                            if(app.dinamica(i)==1)
                                dina(length(dina)+1)=i;
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if(length(app.dinamicae)>0)
                        for i=1:length(app.dinamicae)
                            if(app.dinamicae(i)==1)
                                dina2(length(dina2)+1)=i;
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    for(i=1:length(app.nomee))
                        fprintf(fileID,'======= %s =======\n\n',app.nomee(i));
                        if(not(ismember(i,dina)))
                            fprintf(fileID,'A análise dinâmica não foi realizada nesse par de engrenagens\n\n');
                        else
                            if(string(app.tipoe{app.refe{i}(1)}(app.refe{i}(2))) == "Dentes Retos" || string(app.tipoe{app.refe{i}(1)}(app.refe{i}(2))) == "Helicoidal")
                                fprintf(fileID,'Coeficientes de segurança do pinhão\n\n');
                                fprintf(fileID,'Contra fadiga: %.2f\n', app.Sfp(i));
                                fprintf(fileID,'Contra escoamento: %.2f\n', app.Shp(i));
                                if(app.Sfp(i)>(app.Shp(i))^2)
                                    fprintf(fileID,'Falha no pinhão proveniente de ESCOAMENTO\n\n');
                                else
                                    fprintf(fileID,'Falha no pinhão proveniente de FADIGA\n\n');
                                end
                                fprintf(fileID,'Coeficientes de segurança da coroa\n\n');
                                fprintf(fileID,'Contra fadiga: %.2f\n', app.Sfg(i));
                                fprintf(fileID,'Contra escoamento: %.2f\n', app.Shg(i));
                                if(app.Sfg(i)>(app.Shg(i))^2)
                                    fprintf(fileID,'Falha na coroa proveniente de ESCOAMENTO\n\n');
                                else
                                    fprintf(fileID,'Falha na coroa proveniente de FADIGA\n\n');
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    for(i=1:length(app.nomeex))
                        fprintf(fileID,'======= %s =======\n\n',app.nomeex(i));
                        if(not(ismember(i,dina2)))
                            fprintf(fileID,'A análise dinâmica não foi realizada nesse eixo\n\n');
                        else
                            if(app.sistema==1)
                                fprintf(fileID,'Diâmetro mínimo: %.2f%s\n',app.dfe(i)*1000,unid2);
                            else
                                fprintf(fileID,'Diâmetro mínimo: %.2f%s\n',app.dfe(i),unid2);
                            end
                            if(app.critf(i)==1)
                                fprintf(fileID,'Falha no eixo devido à FADIGA\n\n');
                            elseif(app.critf(i)==2)
                                fprintf(fileID,'Falha no eixo devido ao ESCOAMENTO\n\n');
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end    
            end
            
                
            fprintf(fileID,'=======================================================');
            fclose(fileID);
            
            fid=fopen('relatorio.txt');
            tline=fgetl(fid);
            t=[];
            while ischar(tline)
                t{length(t)+1}=string(tline);
                tline=fgetl(fid);
            end
            app.TextArea.Value=t
            app.TextArea.Visible='on';




        end

        % Button pushed function: AdicionarDadosButton_2
        function AdicionarDadosButton_2Pushed(app, event)
            nomes = [];
            for i=1:length(app.butte)
                nomes = [nomes string(app.butte(i).Text)];
            end
            ind = find(nomes == string(app.ElementosDropDown.Value));
            app.dinamicae(ind)=1;
            Sy2=app.Sy(ind);
            if(app.sistema==0)
                Sy2=Sy2*6894.76;
            end
            Sut=app.Sutf.Value*1e6;
            if(app.sistema==0)
                Sut=Sut*6.89476;
            end
            tipokat=acharindice(app,app.TratamentosuperficialDropDown);
            crit=acharindice(app,app.CritriodefalhaDropDown);
            tc=app.TempEditField_2.Value;
            if(app.sistema==0)
                tc=(tc-32)/1.8;
            end
            conf=app.ConfEditField_2.Value;
            Ma=app.Mrmax(ind);
            Tm=app.Tmax(ind);
            if(app.sistema==0)
                Ma=Ma*0.112985;
                Tm=Tm*0.112985;
            end
            Mm=0;
            Ta=0;
            n2=app.ns(ind);
            d2=0.05;
            [nf,nf2]=deixo(d2,Ma,Tm,Mm,Ta,Sut,tipokat,tc,conf,Sy2);
            if(nf>n2 && nf2>n2)
                while(nf>n2 && nf2>n2)
                    d2=d2-0.0001;
                    [nf,nf2]=deixo(d2,Ma,Tm,Mm,Ta,Sut,tipokat,tc,conf,Sy2);
                end
            else
                while(nf<n2 || nf2<n2)
                    d2=d2+0.0001;
                    [nf,nf2]=deixo(d2,Ma,Tm,Mm,Ta,Sut,tipokat,tc,conf,Sy2);
                end
            end
            if(app.sistema==1)
                app.dfe(ind)=d2;
            else
                app.dfe(ind)=d2*1000/25.4;
            end
            if(nf<nf2)
                app.critf(ind)=1;
            else
                app.critf(ind)=2;
            end
            
            
            function [nf,nf2]= deixo(d2,Ma,Tm,Mm,Ta,Sut,tipokat,tc,conf,Sy2)
                sigmaa=((32*Ma/(pi*d2^3))^2+3*((16*Ta)/(pi*d2^3))^2)^(1/2);
                sigmam=((32*Mm/(pi*d2^3))^2+3*((16*Tm)/(pi*d2^3))^2)^(1/2);
            
            
                %Sel
            
                if(Sut<1400e6)
                    Sel=0.5*Sut;
                else
                    Sel=700;
                end
                % Ka
            
            
                kat=[1.34 1.58 -0.085;
                     2.7 4.51 -0.265;
                     14.4 57.7 -0.718;
                     39.9 272  -0.995];
            
                 ka=kat(tipokat,2)*(Sut/(1e6))^kat(tipokat,3);
            
                 % Kb
            
                 if(d2<0.051)
                     kb=((d2*1000)/7.62)^(-0.107);
                 else
                     kb=1.51*(d2*1000)^(-0.157);
                 end
            
                 % Kc
            
                 kc=1;

                 % Kd
            
                 kd=0.9877+0.6507e-3*tc-0.3414e-5*tc^2+0.5621e-8*tc^3-6.246e-12*tc^4;
            
                 % Ke
            
                 if(conf<=0.9)
                     ke=1-(conf-0.5)/(0.9-0.5)*(1-0.897);
                 elseif(conf<=0.95)
                     ke=0.897-(conf-0.9)/(0.95-0.9)*(0.897-0.868);
                 elseif(conf<=0.99)
                     ke=0.868-(conf-0.95)/(0.99-0.95)*(0.868-0.814);
                 elseif(conf<=0.999)
                     ke=0.814-(conf-0.99)/(0.999-0.99)*(0.814-0.753);
                 elseif(conf<=0.9999)
                     ke=0.753-(conf-0.999)/(0.9999-0.999)*(0.753-0.702);
                 elseif(conf<=0.99999)
                     ke=0.702-(conf-0.9999)/(0.99999-0.9999)*(0.702-0.659);
                 elseif(conf<=0.999999)
                     ke=0.659-(conf-0.99999)/(0.999999-0.99999)*(0.659-0.620);
                 end
                
                kf=1;
                Se=ka*kb*kc*kd*ke*kf*Sel;
            
            
                r2=sigmaa/sigmam;
                if(crit==1)
                    nf=1/(sigmaa/Se+sigmam/Sut);
                    Sa=r2*Se*Sut/(r2*Sut+Se);
                    Sm=Sa/r2;
                elseif(crit==2)
                    nf=1/2*(Sut/sigmam)^2*sigmaa/Se*(-1+sqrt(1+(2*sigmam*Se/(Sut*sigmaa))^2));
                    Sm=Sut^2/(2*Se)*(1-sqrt(1+(2*Se/Sut)^2*(1-Sy2/Se)));
                    Sa=Sy2-Sm;
                    rcrit=Sa/Sm;
                elseif(crit==3)
                    nf=sqrt(1/((sigmaa/Se)^2+(sigmam/Sy2)^2));
                    Sa=sqrt(r2^2*Se^2*Sy2^2/(Se^2+r2^2*Sy2^2));
                    Sm=Sa/r2;
                    rcrit=Sa/Sm;
                end
                nf2=Sy2/(sigmam+sigmaa);
            end
            
        end
    end

            app.ConfEditField_2 = uieditfield(app.EixosPanel, 'numeric');
            app.ConfEditField_2.Position = [171 384 52 22];
            app.ConfEditField_2.Value = 0.9;

            % Create AdicionarDadosButton_2
            app.AdicionarDadosButton_2 = uibutton(app.EixosPanel, 'push');
            app.AdicionarDadosButton_2.ButtonPushedFcn = createCallbackFcn(app, @AdicionarDadosButton_2Pushed, true);
            app.AdicionarDadosButton_2.Position = [309 17 104 22];
            app.AdicionarDadosButton_2.Text = 'Adicionar Dados';

            % Create AtualizarButton_2
            app.AtualizarButton_2 = uibutton(app.EixosPanel, 'push');
            app.AtualizarButton_2.Visible = 'off';
            app.AtualizarButton_2.Position = [205 17 100 22];
            app.AtualizarButton_2.Text = 'Atualizar';

            % Create DeletarButton_2
            app.DeletarButton_2 = uibutton(app.EixosPanel, 'push');
            app.DeletarButton_2.Visible = 'off';
            app.DeletarButton_2.Position = [415 17 100 22];
            app.DeletarButton_2.Text = 'Deletar';

            % Create CritriodefalhaDropDownLabel
            app.CritriodefalhaDropDownLabel = uilabel(app.EixosPanel);
            app.CritriodefalhaDropDownLabel.Position = [35 301 94 15];
            app.CritriodefalhaDropDownLabel.Text = 'Critério de falha:';

            % Create CritriodefalhaDropDown
            app.CritriodefalhaDropDown = uidropdown(app.EixosPanel);
            app.CritriodefalhaDropDown.Items = {'Goodman modificado', 'Gerber', 'ASME-Elíptico'};
            app.CritriodefalhaDropDown.Position = [172 297 138 22];
            app.CritriodefalhaDropDown.Value = 'Goodman modificado';

            % Create RelatrioButton
            app.RelatrioButton = uibutton(app.ElementosUIFigure, 'push');
            app.RelatrioButton.ButtonPushedFcn = createCallbackFcn(app, @RelatrioButtonPushed, true);
            app.RelatrioButton.Visible = 'off';
            app.RelatrioButton.Position = [11 543 100 22];
            app.RelatrioButton.Text = 'Relatório';

            % Create Label
            app.Label = uilabel(app.ElementosUIFigure);
            app.Label.HorizontalAlignment = 'right';
            app.Label.Position = [114 626 25 15];
            app.Label.Text = '';

            % Create TextArea
            app.TextArea = uitextarea(app.ElementosUIFigure);
            app.TextArea.Visible = 'off';
            app.TextArea.Position = [152 43 711 600];
        end
    end

    methods (Access = public)

        % Construct app
        function app = TCCv138F

            % Create and configure components
            createComponents(app)

            % Register the app with App Designer
            registerApp(app, app.ElementosUIFigure)

            % Execute the startup function
            runStartupFcn(app, @startupFcn)

            if nargout == 0
                clear app
            end
        end

        % Code that executes before app deletion
        function delete(app)

            % Delete UIFigure when app is deleted
            delete(app.ElementosUIFigure)
        end
    end
end
